BDU D-DUL-RDO-RJE AND GNAM-CHOS
MI-"GYUR-RDO-RJE



Bdud-' dul-rdo-rie
VOLUME I
1) Snyan brgyud rin po che'i mdzod khang: zab mo gter gyi rgyan
'khor las: rtsa ba bsgrub dkyil chi med dpal ster: 'chi
bdag bdud bcom bzhugso
ff. 9 (pp. 1-18)
Terminatur:
/...dpag bsam ljon 'bras rgya chen kun khyab 'di: rtag
brtan rdo rje snying po'i yang rtse ru: kaha thog sprul sku
kun bzang snying po yis: thabs shes rigs lnga'i sgyu 'phrul
las grub pa'i: skal ldan bung ba'i pad tshal rgyas par shog:
sarba mangga lam:
2) Sayan rgyud rin po che'i mdzod khang zab mo gter gyi rgyan
'khor las: dbang chog ye yin ngang rdzogs sku bzhi Ihun grub
gser gyi mchod sdong bdud bzhi dpung bcoms bzhugso
ff. 8 (pp. 19-34)
Terminatur:
/...phyogs med phyogs bral nam mkha'i khyon yangs pa:
mal 'byor nus ldan rdo rje blo bde'i bkod: rtag brtan rdo
rje snying po'i yang rtse ru: kah thog sprul sku kun bzang
snying po yis: thabs shes rigs lnga'i sgyu 'phrul 'phrul
las grub: skal ldan bung ba'i pad tshal rgyas par shog:
mangga lam:
3) Rig 'dzin grub pa'i dbang phyug 7 bdud 'dul rdo rje'i mam
thar gter 'byung mdor bsdus dad pa'i mchod sdong zhes by a
ba bzhugs so
ff. 25 (pp. 35-84)
Terminatur:
/zhes rig 'dzin grub pa'i dbang phyug bdud 'dul rdo
rje'i ram thar gter 'byung mdor bsdus dag pa'i mchod sdong
zhes bya ba/ rje de nyid kyi zhabs rdul spyi bor len pa'i
sngags btsun stag ras pa kun bzang padma bio ldan gyis ba
khrod smin grol chos lding gi gtsug lag khang chen por
bkod pa dge'o /
4) Kho bo Rig 'dzin Bdud 'dul rdo rje yi: dag snang yid bzhin
nor bu dbang gi rgyal po skyo sangs ma zhes bya ba bzhugs

Bdud-'dul-rdo-rie (1615-1672 or 1627-1684)
Rig 'dzin grub pa'i dbang phyug bdud 'dul rdo rje'i mam thar
gter 'byung mdor bsdus dad pa'i mchod sdong zhes bya ba bzhugs
so
lan
ff. 25 (pp. 35-84 in v. 1 of the collected works, 1984)
Author: Stag-ras-pa Kun-bzang-padma-blo-ldan
/zhes rig 'dzin grub pa'i dbang phyug bdud 'dul rdo rje'i
ram thar gter 'byung mdor bsdus dad pa'i mchod sdong zhes bya
ba/ rje de nyid kyi zhabs rdul spyi bor len pa'i sngags btsun
stag ras pa kun bzang padma blo ldan gyis ba khrod smin grol
chos lding gi gtsug lag khang chen por bkod pa dge'o/



/na mo badzra gu ru ma ra dzi tam bhyah/
/gdod nas lhun grub sbub la nang gsal mngon par byang
chub chos kyi sku/
/rang gdangs phyi gsal zhi dang khro sogs dkyil 'khor 'khor
lo longs spyod rdzogs/
/gang 'dul der snang byin rlabs mchog dang ye shes dam pa
sprul pa'i sku/
/rang bzhin 'gro 'dul gzugs sku'i gar mdzad gangs de baud
dul rdo rje rtsal/
7de yi zhabs sen od zer rtsibs stong pal
/bdag lus shar ri'i gtsug na lham mer 'khod/
/g.yo med dad rgyas btud de gang de yi)
/mam thar gter 'byung cha tsam reg zer bri/
/de yang grub pa'i dbang phyug de la mtshan gyi mam
grangs ji snyed pa zhig rgyal tshab dam par mnga' gsol ba'i
bab rim gyis 'byung ba yin tel padma gar dbang rtsal (f. lv)



Bdud-'dul-rdo-rie
gter bzhed snying po/ bdud 'dul gling pal bdud dul rdo rje/
gar dbang ting 'dzin bzang po/ gter smyon gling pa/ mal byor
nus ldan rdo rje/ nan mkha'i mal 'byor seng ge rtsal rdzogs
la sogs rgyal thebs chen po'i spyi blug 'chang ba'i cha nas
tha dad pa'i mtshan du mar 'byung bar yin nal de yang 'di skad
thos te/ thang yig la/
gter kha mang mthun lung gi zin la bya/ zhes byung ba'i/
'di nyid snga phyi'i gter lung rnams nas ji Itar lung bstan
pa'i tshul ni/ gter ston gru gu yang dbang gi gter lung las/
dus ngan tha ma bstan pa mar 'grib dus/
bod khams bde ba ntha' ma'i dpung gis 'joms/
ri bo re la sngar med btsan rdzongs brtsegs/
de tshe (f. 2r)



sangs rgyas nus ldan rdo rje ni
/shar gyi phyogs nas nus ldan rdo rje yis
/gangs can bde ba'i bya las sna tshogs bsgrubs/ /zhes dang/
gu ru chos kyi dbang phyug gi gter lung las/
shar nas stag yos lo pa la
/gdong rme can 'byung snying gi bu zhes dange
gter ston lha btsun sngon mo'i gter lung las/
bod khams kun tu ntha' ma'i 'ur rgyug byed) zhes dang/
gter ston ratna gling pa'i 'gter lung las/
rdo rje'i ming (bdud 'dul rdo rje) can thugs kyi mtshan ma
can/
/khams phyogs gnas kyi phyogs nas 'byung/
/rdo rje'i (mi 'gyur rdo rje) ming can ngom gyi phyogs nas
'byung/
/nor bu'i ming can khams kyi lho phyogs 'byung/ zhes dang/
gter ston rdo rje gling pa'i gter lung las/
slob dpon hum chen ka ra nyid
/khams kyi phyogs nas bdud 'dul rdo rje zhes
/mngon spyod drag po'i zhing bcu'i gdug pa 'dul/ /zhes dang/
gter (f. 2v)



Bdud-'dul-rdo-rie
ston dri med lhun po'i dan tig 'gro ba kun 'grol nas/
stag yos lo pa badzra shri'i ming/
/tshangs skud me bas spras pa'i skyes bu 'byung/ /zhes
dang/ gter ston o rgyan gling pa dang/ sangs rgyas gling pa
dang/ padma gling pa gsum gyi padma bka! thang las/
bdud 'dul rdo rje lung bstan pa/
/tshe lo bzhi bcu pa la dgra yi bskal pa dar/
mi mams tshe thung nad mang blo bur 'chi/
/gdon du pho gdon klu dang 'byung po gdon/
/bud med mo lus thob tshad gson 'dre gdon/
/thog dang sa g.yos dmag dang mu ge ' byung/
/khrims 'jig yul 'tshug gnam pa go log byung/
/de tshe pad 'byung sprul pa shar gyi phyogs nas 'byung/
zhes dang/ gter ston ma ti ratna'i gter lung las/
mdo khams orgyan rdzu 'phrul gsang phug rams:
khye'u chung lo tsā'i sprul pas 'byed par 'gyur: zhes
dang/ gter ston mi 'gyur rdo rje'i (f. 3r)



gam chos las:
gter ston bdud 'dul rdo rje 'di:
rje 'bangs khe'u chung 10 tså yin: zhes dang/ gter ston
rin chen gling pa'i zab chos nor bu bskor gsum lung byang Ias:
de tshe sangs rgyas nus ldan rdo rje ni:
khams kyi phyogs nas nus ldan rdo rje zhes:
sbas yul padma bkod pa'i gnas sgo 'byed: zhes sogs rgya
cher gsungs shing: sog bzlog pa blo gros bzang pos orgyan
mam thar du/
gter ston nus ldan rdo rje zhes khams kyi gter gas brgya
rtsa 'byed pa zhig 'ong bar thang yig mying pa 'ga' zhig las
'byung ba/ de nas dus rtags la sogs ding sang gi skabs yin par
'dug kyang de sngon ma byon pa ci/ 'gro ba'i bsod nams kyis
ma thob pa yin nam) zhes gsungs pa dang/ de bzhin du dpa' bo
gtsug lag phreng bas mying ma chos 'byung du:
mal 'byor nus ldan rdo rje zhes khams kyi gter sgo 'byed
pa zhig (f. 3v)



Bdud-' dul-rdo-rje
'ong bar thang yig gcig na 'dug pa ni da Ita'i dus yin par
snyam mo/ zhes gsungs pa la sogs snga phyi'i gter lung du ma
nas lung bstan pa'i skyes chen dam pa som nyi med pa lags so/
./de yang chos kyi sku las ma g.yos bzhin du gzugs sku'i
mam par 'phrul pa bsam gyis mi khyab pa 'gro ba'i don mdzad
pa la 'di rhes pa'i tshad bzung bar mi nus mod/ 'on kyang cung
zad brjod na/ de yang thog mar sangs rgyas stong rtsa gnyis la
dbang bskur zhing lung bstan mdzad pa sangs rgyas nus Idan rdo
rjel thub pa'i spyan sngar dgra bcom nye rgyal zhes/ shā ri'i
bu/ u rgyan rgyal po'i chos blon kr pa 'dzin rgya gar gyi grub
chen ham ka ra/ de nyid kyi sprul pa gsum 'gyed de/ slob dpon
padma'i dus su/ sku yi sprul pa gnyags dznyå na ku ma ra/ gsung
gi sprul pa lha sras mu tig btsad pol thugs kyi sprul pa 'brog
ban chye'u chung lo (f, 4r)



tsā sprul pa rim par/ u rgyan yul du dznyā na shwa ra/ pani
chen smri ti/ sa skya'i bsod nams rtse mod khar chen dunyai
na kirti/ rgyal sras bsod nams grags pa/ grub thob khyung po
mal 'byor/ grub thob glang ru thang pa) 'gro mgon chos rgyal
'phags pa/ blo gros dpal bzang pol rgya gar na lan dar pan chen
buddha ratna/ grub chen gling ras padma rdo rjel rtsa sde
zhwa nag pa) spyan sngar nam mkha" rdo rje/ grub thob gcer
sgom pa/ rgya gar du ka ra ka ti badzra) gtsang nas mal 'byor
dkar po pal yar stod pa sde pa lha dbang zhes las 'phro gling
pa'i chos bdag/ bka' sman tshe bstan zhes padma gling pas
chos bdag/ gter ston bde chen rol pa rtsal/ zhig po/ bde chen
mnga che/ kun dga' 'bum zhes/ ratna'i slob ma grub thob mkhar

5
bla ma chos kyi 'byung gnas/ de nyid rig 'dzin chen por snang
nas bstan 'gro'i dpal du shar ba'o/
/ma 'ongs pa'i sangs rgyas Inga pa me tog zhes phyi ma
nyid du 'gyur bar gsungs sol
/de Ita bu'i skyes chen dam pa de nyid sku bltams pa'i
yum ni/ shar phyogs mdo khams dpal kah thog pa'i cha 'bri chu
dal 'bab kyi giyon/ bde dge pho brang gi mnga' ris/ zul chu'i
rgyud 'bri gnyen 'dong rdo rje blo gros kyi gnas dang nye ba
rgyang mda'i pho brang gi phu rào thang zhes bye bar rus chen
smug po gdong/ rigs gling yin te ge sar skyes bu don grub
kyi gdung rigs/ yab 'tsho byed klu skyabs zhes pa®i sras su
me yos (1627) la sku bl tams dgung lo drug nas dag pa'i snang
ba bsam gyis mi khyab cing zhabs rjes bzhag/ 'di Ita bu ni
dpag tu med pa'i sngon nas sbyangs pa'i yon tan mthar son
pa yin na'ang/ gzhan dag la yon tan gyi che ba ston pa'i phyir
yab (f. 5r)
b. 1627



las 'bri klog gi gso ba mthar phyin pa mdzad: rang rig bla
mar gyur kyang dge ba'i bshes gnyen bsten dgos par gzhan la
ston pa'i phyir/ bde dge grub thob kun (dgongs pa yongs 'dus
kyi/ sngon dus sa skya zhabs drung mthu stobs la gtsug phud
phul/ rgyal tshab kyi rgyud las spyan ras gzigs sprul gu ru'i
ming zhig dang 'phrad nas dgongs don rtogs gyur kyang/ bar
chad mang du ' byung bar 'gyur/zhes so/) dga' rgya mtsho las
rab tu byung ste/ mtshan kun dga' bsod nams chos 'phags su
gsol/ de nas nye bar mtshan ldan gu ru seng ha'i drung du/
gdams khrid yongs su rdzogs pa gsan/
rmug sangs gnas su byon nas bya btang tra ya seng ha
la'ang/ smin grol bskyed rdzogs kyi gdams pa mnos te mthar
phyin par mdzad/
de nas dbus gtsang gi phyogs su byon te/ kong po lcags sde
grub thob pa gter ston bkra shis tshe bstan la rang bzhin
rdzogs pa chen po'i smin grol bskyed rdzogs thams cad bum pa
gang byo'i tshul du mnos (f. 5v)

shing/ brag dkar lha chur zab lam rtsa rlung thig le'i mal

mdzad/

de 'phrad nyams rtogs gong du 'phel/
lung bstan brda' zur 'phrod par 'gyur) zhes gsungs pa

telles
7
1655/56
kha byang lde mig/ zhal gdams rin chen phreng ba/ myong grol
dkar chag reg pa rang grol gsum/ myong grol ril bu mang zhig
byon/ der bsgrub pa nan du mdzad del
nyer dgu sum bcu (1655-1656) la ide mig la byung ba bzhin/
spu ri bde chen gsang ba phug par rje nyid dang/ dpon 'ja' mo
nye mas o rgyan rgya ntsho la sogs dpon slob gyis phyi nang
tshogs 'khor bskang gsol rgyas par mdzad do/
egter gyi lde mig Itar btsal bas 'phral du myed de/ dpon
slob mams kyis brkos par brag gi ngogs pa rdo mang po'i khrod
na rdo sgrom ltar sgrigs pa'i nang nas shug pa'i shun pa mang
po don byung/ slar yang brkos par sol ba mang po'i dkyil nas/
gter sgrom dam 'be sbrul mgo can/ orgyan rin po che'i sku
tshabs gnam lcags rdo rje dam rdzas myong groi mang zhig byung
ste/ de ma thag sa phyogs dri bzang gi ngad pas khyab/ sku tshab
nyid kyi mam phrag tu (f. 7r)



bzhugs/ gter sgrom la sogs bswe yi rgam du dar snas dril te
reyab tu khur bcol nas brag gi logs bgrod dka' bzhin du phyin
pas/ rten sgam gyi lung thag chad de brag gi rtsa bar lhung
slar yang goyang par 'gril nas song ba/ dpon slob mans kyis
bskor nas tshol du phyin pas/ phyi yi sgam de yang ma zhig la/
nang du gcig kyang ma gnod par byon/ khyin du gter sgrub byas
shog ser bshu ba'i lta gon la zhugs/
tshes bcu mdzad pa na slong tshad cher byung ste/ 'khor
mams la bka' bkyon gang/ bdag 1ta buli o rgyan rin po ches
bstan pa la bya ba byed nus sam/ 'di 'dra na shog ser 'di
dag zhal mi bshu bar slar gter du sba 'gro ba yin gsungs nas
bzhengs/ 'khor mams kyis nan tan du gsol ba btab pas bzhugs
te zhal bshu bar bkas gnang/ shog ser zhal bshus gter tshabs
bzhag/
de dus kyi shug shun dang sol ba 'ga' zhig dpon (f. 7v)



Bdud-'dul-rdo-rie
'ja' mot thogs yong ba zho chang bokur ba la cung Zad re btab
pas shin tu phan pa chen po byung ngo/
/dam chos 'di nyid gter kha kun gyi snga shos yin pas phyis
bton pa mnams kyi cho ga'i yan lag ma tshang ba la sogs 'di
nyid nas kha bkang bar mdzad zhes rig 'dzin chen po'i gsungs so/
/lam du nam mkha' nas mkha' 'gro sde bzhi byung ste rdo
rje rgya gro(gram?) gyi steng du bzhag nas phyogs bzhir dar yug
btags pa btogs nas zangs mdog dpal rir spyan drangs/
rig 'dzin chen po padma 'byung gnas kyi drung du zhag
nyi shu rtsa brgyad bzhugs pa'i snang ba byung ste de dag ni
dag snang yid bzhin nor bu skyo sangs mar gsal 10/
Ide nas dgung lo nyer brgyad (1654) la goyu ntsho rin chen
brag nas dgongs pa yongs 'dus kyi kha byang byung/
nyer dgu (1655) la de nyid spyan drangs/
yang lo gnyis gsum tsam zhig nas mdo smad tsha ba sgro brag
tu (f. 8v)

byon nas sprul sku snying thig spyan drangs/
slar spu bor phebs te dgung lo so Inga glang gi lo (1661)

thig spyan drangs/

bzhes/ rgyal sras nor bu yongs grags sku bltams/
gzhan yang gnas sgo 'ga' dang gter yang mang rab 'don
zhing bsgrub pa dang thugs dam la brtson pa las mi lhod par
yun du bzhugs pa las/ bde dge grub thob kun dga' rgya mtsho
dang/ bla ma kun dga' phun tshogs Sku mched mams kyis yang
nas yang du zhus te/ dgung lo zhe gyis bzhes pa'i me spre'u

Bdud-'dul-rdo-rie
'ba' rang yan zhabs kyis bcag/ gdul bya dang mdzad 'phrin nam
mkha' khyab gdal du 'phel:
slar gyi yul nas dga' gser kha/ 'dan chos 'khor mams su
theg/ sog po kun dga' thal ji'i gdan 'dren zhus pas ma phebs/
tshur drung du 'bul nod rgya chen po mdzad/
de nas ma lha steng la sogs ngom chu'i phur byon) gter
ston mi 'gyur rdo rje dang mjal 'phrad mdzad/ phan tshun gter
gsar abang lung phul te mdzad/
de dus mkhas btsun bzang gsum dge ba'i bshes gnyen du mas
yongs su bskor ri bo cher phyag phebs/ 'tshog pa mams lapse
ratna'i phur pa yang gsang bla med kyi dbang lung gnang/
de nas tsha ba sgang du chag phebs/ dpon dgra lha rgyal
dang rten 'brel gyi legs tshogs 'grig/ de dag gi lam rams su
khyung po rta shod nas bon gter ston/ rtse drug gnas sgo (f.
9r)



mdo khams o rgyan gsang phug/ ru thog gnas/ na bun rdzongs/
khro zil khrom gas la sogs pa'i gnas sgo du ma zhal phyes
shing chos gter dam rdzas bsam gyis mi khyab pa spyan drangs/
phyogs kyi dge ba'i bshes gnyen du mas bskor zhing/ yul mi
dpon blon skya ser che phra thams cad ryis mchod pa'i bye
brag ci 'byor pas mched de/ ri klung kun sgar gzhigs kyis
mngon par gang ba'i 'byor pa dang bcas te/ rgyu dngos de dag
kyang chud zos ma song bar dgon sde che chung thams cad la
'bul 'gyed/ yig drug rgyun 'dzug/ bum bsgrub/ sman bsgrub/
zhal thang/ phyag dpe bzhengs ba/ pad mkhar yan chad kyi rtsa
bar gtong zhing/ skabs 'gar ser skya yul mi skal ba ldan pa
du ma yis/ zla ba gcig gyis tsam du 'od gsal rdo rje snying
po'i khrid btab pa yang lan 'ga' mdzad de thams cad kun bzang
bde ba chen po'i sa (f. 9v)



Bdud-' dul-rdo-rie
10
la 'god par mdzad del de nas rim gyis gdul bya mams la chos
kyi 'khor lo bskor ching spu stod bde chen thang du chags
phebs stel slob ma'i tshogs rgya mtsho lta bu la smin grol
dbang gdams kyi nyin mtshan 'da' bar mdzad cing/ shog ser mnams
kyang ji snyed pa zhig zhal bshu bar mdzad do
/de'i dus bsam yas kyi zhing skyong dpe har rgyal po'i
sku bab byung dus/ rig 'dzin chen po 'dir phebs dgos tshul la
sogs pa gsungs/ dbus gtsang ru bzhi mnga' ris kyi bar grags
par gyur tel de dag gi bla dpon thams cad kyi zhu yig 'bul
skyel thugs dam brtag pa zhu ba'i bang chen du ma rdzong
bar gyur/
lhag par po tā la nas rgyal ba thams cad mkhyen pa blo
bzang chos kyi rgya mtsho'i drung nas lha sa bsam yas su pheb
dgos pa yang yang bskul zhing/ rje sa skya zhabs drung nas
kyang phebs don zhu zhing/ skyi shod zhabs drung rdo (f. 10r)



rje mam rgyal dpon blon mams kyis kyang phebs zhus dang/ bsam
yas kyi chos skyong chen po'i kyang phebs dgos pa'i lam bsrung
gi ral gri zhags pa la sogs bskur nas yang yang zhus pa yin
na'ang/ ma dag pa'i skye bo 'ga' zhig gis snga phyi gsol ba
ngan pa lan gsum bzhi drangs pas sku la gnod pa ma byung bar
rdo rje'i 'khrul 'khor gyi dngos po de nyid dngos su phyir
'byin par mdzad kyang/ de'i dug rlangs gi spyan gyis cher cher
sgrib pas/ de'i stobs kyis pheb par ma mdzad kyang/ de dag
thams cad dang bka' shog zhu skyel yas man du rgyun ma chad
du 'bul zhing/ chos gter mans kyang mthargyas su gyur to!
Ide nas sngon gyi gter lung rnams nas lung bstan pa dang/
nyid kyi spu bo 'dong chu 1ha khang nas padma bkod kyi gmas
yig bton par mdzad pa ltar/ sbas yul padma bkod kyi gnas sgo
'byed pa lung bstan pa las byung pa'i phyag rgya mo dpon ob
(f. 10v)

Bdud-'dul-rdo-rje
Dam chos Dgongs pa yong 'dus
Gur-phu-ba Nor-bu-bde-chen's Gsan yig, pp. 16-24
/yang DGONGS PA YONGS 'DUS kyi bla ma'i las byang don
gyi gsal byed/ sgrub chen spra khrid khyung chen Iding ba/
sgrubs chen byin 'bebs yid bzhin nor bu/ sgrub chen gyi cha
lag bdud rtsi sman gyi bskul byang bgegs dpung kun 'joms
mams rang lo zhe Inga Icags mo glang (1661) drug cu skor
11 pa'i nang tshan (born 1617) (p. 16) lo rgyal ba ma bdun
ras chen gyi sgrub gnas chos rdzong ri khrod du thugs rje
dges pa chen pos/ stsal ba dge legs su gyur cig/
/yang sprul pa'i gter bton chen po BDUD 'DUL DPAL GYI
RDO RJEs/ spu ri bde chen gsang phug nas spyan drangs pa'i
zab chos bka' rdzogs pa chen po DAM CHOS DGONGS PA YONGS
'DUS kyi chos skor yongs rdzogs thob pa la bdun las/ lo rgyus
stong thun gyi skor/ smin byed dbang gi skor/ sgrub thabs

Bdud-'dul-rdo-rje
Dam chos Sprul sku snying thig
att det
Gur-phu-ba Nor-bu-bde-chen's Gsan yig, pp. 3-16
/bdag cag gi rje btsun dam pa sbas pa'i rnal 'byor 'di
nyid/ rdo rje slob dpon chen po padma sa mbha was/ snub ban
sangs rgyas ye shes kyi sku'i skye ba yin par lung gis bstan tel
de yang sprul pa'i gter bton chen po BDUD 'DUL DPAL GYI RDO RJE'i
zab gter snying thig zhal lung las/
snub ban sangs rgyas ye shes skye ba snga ris nas:
dpal gyi ming can sme ba'i ga zha can:
padma bdag mos rnal 'byor pa cig 'byung:
'brel tshad don ldan de la chos 'di sprod:
rang gzhan don 'grub mga yab gling du bde: zhes lung gis
bstan pa'i mal 'byor gyi dbang phyug chen po 'di nyid dan chos
sprul sku snying thig gi chos bdag tu mnga' gsol ba/ don gyi (p.
3) slad du mtshan nas smos pa/ DAM CHOS DPAL BZANG PO'am/ 0
RGYAN DPAL BZANG PO zhes mkhas shing grub pa'i mchog brnyes pa'i
yongs 'dzin dam pa mang po'i zhabs sen la reg pas) zab cing rgya
che ba'i smin grol chos kyi bdul rtsibi ro mehog ngom pa med pa'i
dga' ston la longs spyod pas/ de dag gi tshig don ma lus pa thugs
kyi klong du mngon par byang chub stel ji Ita ba dang ji snyed
pa'i mkhyen rtogs kyi nus pa phul du phyin pa'i grub pa'i dbang
phyug chen po gang de'i zhal snga nas/ gsang chen bla na med pa'i
smin grol gi zab chos ji snyed cig bka' drin du stsal ba las/
thog mar/ 'brog ban dpal gyi ye shes bsam bzhin du sku'i skye
ba bzhes pa sprul pa'i gter bton chen po RIG 'DZIN BDUD 'DUL
DPAL GYI RDO RJEs/ shar phyogs mdo khams kyi gnas tsha ba sgro
brag ban ri padma 'od kyi ghu ru'i gsang phug nas gdan drangs
pa'i gsang gter DAM CHOS SPRUL SKU SNYING THIG gi chos skor
thob pa la rnam grangs bdun te/*khungs btsun lo rgyus kyi skor/(p. 4)*
smin lam dbang gi skor/ grol lam bskyed rdzogs kyi skor/ 'gro
'dul las tshogs kyi skor/ dus gsum lung bstan gyi skor/ bka'
bsrung chos skyong gi skor/ bka' nyan gter bsrung gi skor ro/
/dang po khungs btsun lo rgyus kyi skor la/
1) Dag snang yid bzhin nor bu dbang gi rgyal po skyo sangs ma
zhes bya ba/

thabs mun sel sgron me/

/chos nyid bden pa mngon sum mthong bar shog/
